<userid>111084687796954819116< /userid><username>Eniko Nagy</username><Time>1564409085806</Time><Rate>5<//Rate>< Review>
Took a day trip to Balch Park and stayed around the lake while my son was fishing and my daughter and toddler were hunting for frogs. I love to watch the ducks on the lake and hearing the deep croaks of the frogs. It's a beautiful place and there is a lot for kids to explore and trails to walk. Dogs are allowed on a leash. We went on a Sunday and it was not crowded at all. It was a fun day.</Review>

<Text>Very beautiful scenery. Loved how peaceful it felt around campsites. Campsites had tent and RV sites with hookups. Bathrooms were nearby campsites throughout the park. Each site had bear boxes and courtesy trash bins. There were camp hosts there, as well as running water, and electric hookups. The road going up there was not kept up very well, and was a bit winding. The camp hosts had travel trailers, so I assume you can haul one up there.  Going back down the mountain the opposite way was beautiful, but it took a little bit longer. I preferred going through balch park road instead; which was the opposite way.<//Text><user_id>110361018628047280889</user_id></record></dataset><record>

< text>
I have utilized Vetmatrix for two different companies.  I have had two incredibly different experiences.

My Vetmatrix team was amazing the first time around the block.  They never became defensive, showed me numerous options for design, and always seemed willing to help out in any manner possible.  This team deserved five stars.

Five years passed.  I started managing a new company and gave them a call for service.  Their company must have exploded.  I sincerely think they are struggling to keep up with business.

I definitely would not recommend this company currently.  The only reason I am still a client of Vetmatrix is because the website is finished, and I do not want to go through this hassle again with another company.

The social media package will not allow you to preview or tailor posts.  You get to see them at the same time as the general public.  The website design will absolutely take a month or longer.  Response time is 48 business hours via email and sometimes by phone.

Some technicians do not understand aesthetics and genuinely struggle to make your designs.  Be very direct and literal when describing how you want something to be designed.

They are incredibly affordable, and our website does look amazing after two months of design, but I do not feel like a valued client or account.  Our account is expendable.<//text>

<Time>1493914561818</Time>< Review>
First, I should start by saying that I am a very picky shopper. I shop around, I do my research, I check online for other vendors with better deals before committing to a purchase. Especially a large purchase, a purchase I don't plan on making again for several years to come - like furniture!

I checked what Target, Buy Buy Baby and Babies R' Us offer. I also browsed several small furniture stores and online vendors. At the end of the day, I found that Babies R' Us had good quality furniture pieces at the best prices, and a lot on display - I like being able to see furniture in person before buying! They also tend to have good sales, so I kept my eye out for specials.

But what really made me a fan was the customer service. Granted, I think I got very lucky having bumped into RICHARD GALLARDO. He works at the Mira Mesa location and defines what good customer service is or should be. He surpasses it. I was looking for a furniture set that seemed to be sold out (the crib and dresser were, the bookshelf was available, some of the conversion kits were sold out as well). Richard made sure to call every store in the district, to gather each and every piece that I was looking to buy. He literally spent about 3-4 hours the first night I walked into Babies R' Us to make sure I would get everything I needed, and in a timely manner. It did take about a month for all the pieces to come in, but he communicated with me the entire time, we even text, and now I have the beautiful nursery I had imagined! Honestly, I am fairly certain most other stores would have simply said, sorry, this set is sold out! Probably would have tried to sell me on something else!

Richard also gave me advice on several other pieces, that as a first time mom, I had not considered purchasing or known about. Not necessarily expensive things, I didn't feel like I was being sold (I am in sales myself so I especially hate being sold!). He recommended a baby swing, which he mentioned his own son really enjoyed - and gave me a few pointers on how to select a good one. He also mentioned a backseat mirror to calm the baby in the car (since the new CA law says babies should be backward facing for 2 years and if they fuss, you can't simply see them through your back view mirror). He made sure everything I purchased, was purchased off my registry - so I would get all the points I had earned (I didn't even know these points existed, but he told me I needed to get them to make sure I got a nice check after the delivery of the baby!).

All in all, shopping at Babies R' Us, with Richard, was a pleasant experience. The communication and patience and assistance he offered will certainly bring me back to the Mira Mesa location!!! In fact, I recommend you ask for Richard when you get to the store, especially if you are looking to make a big purchase and need someone you can trust to help you along.</Review>

They also have 2 different SKU numbers for parts made in America, Canada, or Japan... but they also have SKU numbers for those that are made elsewhere; again so they can appeal to the more frugal customer.\n\nAnd of course if you call the dealer with "Tokyo Auto is charging me $XXX, how much would you charge me to..." then of course they are going to give you the cheaper price. <response>{'time': 1596136060816, 'text': "Suren, I apologize for the loose cable. He was not a new tech, he should've known better. But people make mistakes & he's apologized.\n\nAs for the diagnosis, I've had many times when the tow truck driver was wrong. What the tow truck driver says is often speculation or gut feeling based on the fact it's output is less than 14.3 volts. What our diagnostic does beyond what tow truck driver says is actually looks at computer systems and see if they are commanding the system voltage. Many times especially on a sophisticated system, such as on your RDX, the voltage regulator is external of your alternator. If we just went blindly off what tow truck driver said, it's possible that we might've replaced a perfectly good alternator.\n\nAs for the monies for the diagnosis, we no longer live in a society where milk is 10 cents, especially in Southern California where median house prices are 650K. Things to know before you go:
-Under new management, a majority of these positive reviews are from when Aki was in charge of the business, his son Tatsu now runs the place
-Their labor rate is higher than Weir Canyon Honda's
-They charge a premium on top of MSRP for parts, I mean that very most expensive number you can find for a part, they charge extensively on top of that 50%+ more because "they have a right to make a profit on the parts"....even though there's profit already built into the MSRP because you're buying it at below MSRP....
-Their Diagnosis fee DOES NOT roll into your work, Unlike the dealers. If they say 3 hours of Labor, you're paying for at least 4 because of their diagnosis fee, dealers don't do that. Dealers Hourly rates are cheaper too

Here's the background,
My very first 5 star Yelp review was for Tokyo Automotive many, many, years ago. Since then many things have changed. Aki is no longer in charge of the business, his son Tatsu is and boy oh boy have things changed. I recently took my Honda Civic in to have the Airmix Motor replaced they quoted me upwards of $700, having trusted them before and knowing they were amazing before I assumed I was getting a great price on parts and labor. I even asked if the diagnosis time/fee rolled into the repair total, he said YES! Then charged me an additional hour afterwards. Then after paying I started to do more research about it, I even went as far as to take his part number he replaced to 2 dealerships and asked them to quote me on the part and labor to change it out, without either dealership knowing I had already paid for it. Both dealerships quoted me $280/$300.... Having a good relationship with Tokyo Automotive in the past, I called Tatsu and in a nice way explained to him that I thought he over charged me, I got slammed down with "We have to pay our employees living wages, we don't have people working for $12 an hour" and "Well you get a 3 year warranty with us, you won't get that anywhere else" (3 year warranty when I paid over double up front.... let that sink in) I really was trying to let Tatsu do the right thing but he just wouldn't and that's too bad. Myself, my brother, my grandmother, two aunts, my dad, church friends have all used and loved Tokyo Motors in the past, we've always been impressed by them, but as long as Tatsu's at the helm none of us will be back. I hope he finds his way again and doesn't lose everything his dad built and worked so hard for.

Moral of the story, Tatsu doesn't want want to give you the best service for the best price anymore like his father always strived to do, making a deal on a handshake. His father knew that a repeat loyal customer, who brags about you to all their friends and family so when your friends/family have an issue with their car you speak up and say, "Hey I Know a great guy!" and he gets the business is better way in life. That's the Tokyo Automotive Aki built. Tatsu wants to try to sell you on a great fancy experience of some sort. I thought the dealership is where you pay for an experience, loaner cars, popcorn, soda etc. I've never cared for those kinds of places personally. All I knew was Aki was the man for the job, and I trusted him, what he would do for our cars and our family. To each their own, I wish Tatsu the best of luck, his way of running the business is just not a business I would want to do business with.</Text>

< Text>
Holy Heaven this place was great! I come from Washington state where we have some of the best sushi. Had only room for two rolls but they were fantastic!

Pros:The PJ roll was incredible, good creamy texture from the cream cheese, very decent flavor. My most favorite of the two: The Banana roll: Shrimp Tempura, cream cheese rolled topped with tempura banana and eel sauce (Though I recommend having the sauce on the side like I did, it was good but depending on your taste it may or may not go well with the banana.) Overall impressed with the service, very quick response and friendly!

The dessert I had was YUMMY, fried banana ice cream. Though I recommend staying off the whipped cream. The portion however was decent for two people.

Cons: Careful if you like sucking down coke or iced tea, no free refills, .95/glass, so savor it.

Stars: 4.5 out of 5

Highly recommend this place for those who love sushi.</Text>

The sushi is really good here, fresh and lots of variety. Love the banana roll and the Yesenia roll. It is a nice hidden place, wasn't too busy, and service was quick. (Almost too quick! Felt a little rushed.)

We went here for a date night, and it wasn't bad. My boyfriend ordered a coke, and wish they woulda told us refills weren't free, and were $1.99. He would have gotten water too.

We had a good meal, actually couldn't finish all we got and it was really good.

Set up is a little weird, we were at a booth where there seemed to be a hidden playpen for kids right next to us. A little strange, but cool if you are looking for a corner to hide the kids while you eat.</review>
